create table VENDOR (
	VENDOR_NO int not null,
	NAME VARCHAR(50) null,
        STREET VARCHAR(30),
        CITY VARCHAR(12),
        STATE CHAR(2),
        ZIP int,
	TEL_NO VARCHAR(12) null, 
	constraint VENDOR_PK primary key (VENDOR_NO) ) ;

go 

insert into vendor values	('1000','Samsung','21 Roscoe Dr','Rochester','MN','52010','509 631 2121');
insert into vendor values	('1001','Sony','109 Shepard Dr','Madison','WI','68012','302 241 2121');
insert into vendor values	('1002','Microsoft','310 Simpson Ave','New York','NY','78012','631 241 2121');
 
go

create table PRODVENDOR (
    	PO_NO int not null,
	VENDOR_NO int null,
	PRODUCT_NO int not null,
	ORDER_DATE DATE null,
	EXPECTED_RECVD_DATE DATE null,
	ACTUAL_RECVD_DATE DATE null,
	VEND_QTY int null,
	DPRICE CHAR(10) null,
	CONSTRAINT PRODVENDOR_PO_NO_PK PRIMARY KEY (PO_NO)); 
go

create table ORDERS (
	ORDER_NO int not null,
	ORDER_DATE DATE not null,
	SHIP_DATE DATE null,
	SHIPPING_METHOD VARCHAR(12) null,
	TAX_STATUS CHAR(1) null,
	SUBTOTAL int null,
	TAX_AMT int  null,
	SHIPPING_CHARGE int null,
	TOTAL_AMT int null,
	CUSTOMER_NO int null,
	EMPLOYEE_NO int null,
	BRANCH_NO int null,
	constraint ORDERS_ORDERNO_PK primary key (ORDER_NO) );

create table BRANCH (
	BRANCH_NO int not null,
	STREET VARCHAR(30) null,
	CITY VARCHAR(15) not null,
	STATE VARCHAR(2) ,
        REGION_NO int ,
	ZIP int null constraint BRANCH_ZIP_CHK check ( ZIP > 0 ) , 
	constraint BRANCH_BRANCHNO_PK primary key (BRANCH_NO) );
	
go

CREATE TABLE EMPLOYEE(
EMPLOYEE_NO int not null,
LNAME VARCHAR(12) NOT NULL ,
FNAME VARCHAR(12) ,
STREET VARCHAr(30),
CITY VARCHAR(15),
STATE VARCHAR(2),
ZIP int ,
STATUS int ,
DOB DATE NOT NULL ,
START_DATE  DATE ,
END_DATE DATE ,
BRANCH_NO int NOT NULL ,
BRANCH_SIZE VARCHAR(30),
POSITION int ,
RATE int ,
COMMISSION int ,
CONSTRAINT EMPLOYEE_BRANCH_NO_FK FOREIGN KEY (BRANCH_NO) REFERENCES BRANCH (BRANCH_NO),
CONSTRAINT EMPLOYEE_NO_PK PRIMARY KEY (EMPLOYEE_NO));

CREATE TABLE CUSTOMER(
CUSTOMER_NO int not null,
LNAME VARCHAR(12),
FNAME VARCHAR(12),
STREET VARCHAR(30),
CITY VARCHAR(15),
STATE VARCHAR(2),
ZIP int,
REGION_NO int,
TEL_NO VARCHAR(15) ,
BALANCE int ,
CREDIT_LIMIT int ,
BRANCH_NO int null,	
CONSTRAINT CUST_NUM_PK PRIMARY KEY (CUSTOMER_NO),
CONSTRAINT CUSTOMER_BRANCH_NO_FK FOREIGN KEY (BRANCH_NO) REFERENCES BRANCH (BRANCH_NO)) ;
go

create table regions (
        region_no int not null , 
        timezone varchar(40) ,
        CONSTRAINT regions_pk primary key (region_no));
go
insert into regions values	('1','Hawaiian');

go

create table PRODUCT (
	PRODUCT_NO int not null,
	BRAND VARCHAR(15) null,
	CLASS VARCHAR(20) null,
	PRODUCT_DESCRIPTION VARCHAR(50) null,
	UNIT_PRICE int null,
	UNIT_COST int null,
	PRODUCT_CATEGORY VARCHAR(15) null,
	QOH int null,
	ORDER_LEVEL int null,
	ORDER_QTY int null,
	BACK_ORDER int null,
	AVAIL_DATE DATE null,
	DAMAGED_QTY int null, 
	constraint PRODUCT_PRODUCTNO_PK primary key (PRODUCT_NO) ); 


	ALTER TABLE "PRODVENDOR" ADD CONSTRAINT "PRODVENDOR_VENDOR_NO_FK1" FOREIGN KEY ("VENDOR_NO") REFERENCES  "VENDOR" ("VENDOR_NO") ;
ALTER TABLE "PRODVENDOR" ADD CONSTRAINT "PRODVENDOR_PRODUCT_NO_FK2" FOREIGN KEY ("PRODUCT_NO") REFERENCES  "PRODUCT" ("PRODUCT_NO");
ALTER TABLE "ORDERS" ADD CONSTRAINT "ORDERS_CUSTOMER_NO_FK2" FOREIGN KEY ("CUSTOMER_NO") REFERENCES  "CUSTOMER" ("CUSTOMER_NO") ;
ALTER TABLE "ORDERS" ADD CONSTRAINT "ORDERS_EMPLOYEE_NO_FK3" FOREIGN KEY ("EMPLOYEE_NO") REFERENCES  "EMPLOYEE" ("EMPLOYEE_NO")  ;
ALTER TABLE "ORDERS" ADD CONSTRAINT "ORDERS_BRANCH_NO_FK1" FOREIGN KEY ("BRANCH_NO") REFERENCES  "BRANCH" ("BRANCH_NO")  ;
ALTER TABLE "ORDERLINE" ADD CONSTRAINT "ORDERLINE_PRODUCT_NO_FK2" FOREIGN KEY ("PRODUCT_NO") REFERENCES  "PRODUCT" ("PRODUCT_NO")  ;
ALTER TABLE "ORDERLINE" ADD CONSTRAINT "ORDERLINE_ORDER_NO_FK1" FOREIGN KEY ("ORDER_NO") REFERENCES  "ORDERS" ("ORDER_NO")  ;
ALTER TABLE "BRANCH" ADD CONSTRAINT "BRANCH_REGION_NO_FK1" FOREIGN KEY ("REGION_NO") REFERENCES  "REGIONS" ("REGION_NO")  ;
ALTER TABLE "CUSTOMER" ADD CONSTRAINT "CUSTOMER_REGION_NO_FK2" FOREIGN KEY ("REGION_NO") REFERENCES  "REGIONS" ("REGION_NO")  ;
